Third visit to this place and it keeps getting better each time. We had a dietary requirement and the kitchen adapted beautifully without making it feel like a chore. The quenelles were as light as air - a technically demanding dish executed perfectly.

Restaurant: Wok L
The flavours here are authentic and bold - a lovely change of pace in Lyon. The gyoza had a perfect crispy base and the filling was fragrant and well-balanced. Five stars without a moment's hesitation.
The flavours here are authentic and bold - a lovely change of pace in Lyon. The bao buns were pillowy and the slow-braised filling was rich and deeply savoury. The service struck the perfect balance - present when needed but never hovering unnecessarily. A meal we will be talking about for a long time.
